lang="en"> [#COOKIESIABCONTENT#] </div><div id="CybotCookiebotDialogDetailBodyContentTextAbout" lang="en"> <p class="paragraph" style="margin-top:10px;margin-bottom:10px;box-sizing:border-box;caret-color:#000000;font-family:Avenir-Book;font-size:14px;line-height:22px;">This cookie policy aims to illustrate the cookies type and methods of use on this website.</p><p class="paragraph" style="margin-top:10px;margin-bottom:10px;box-sizing:border-box;caret-color:#000000;font-family:Avenir-Book;font-size:14px;line-height:22px;">Cookies are small size dimension text strings, which the websites visited by the user send to their terminal (usually the browser), where they are stored in order to be re-transmitted to the same sites at the next visit by the same user.</p><p class="paragraph" style="margin-top:10px;margin-bottom:10px;box-sizing:border-box;caret-color:#000000;font-family:Avenir-Book;font-size:14px;line-height:22px;">Kaleyra uses technical cookies, which are those used only for carrying out the transmission of a communication over an electronic communication network, or which are strictly required by for a suppliers from an information society in which it is explicitly requested by the subscriber or by the user to provide the service.</p><p class="paragraph" style="margin-top:10px;margin-bottom:10px;box-sizing:border-box;caret-color:#000000;font-family:Avenir-Book;font-size:14px;line-height:22px;">Particularly Kaleyra uses analytics cookies which are needed to collect information on the number of users and how they visit the website.</p><p class="paragraph" style="margin-top:10px;margin-bottom:10px;box-sizing:border-box;caret-color:#000000;font-family:Avenir-Book;font-size:14px;line-height:22px;">In some cases, cookies that are related to information such as credentials entered for the access to restricted areas (email address and password), can be used to profile the user (personal habits, websites visited, downloaded content, types interactions carried out, etc.).</p><p class="paragraph" style="margin-top:10px;margin-bottom:10px;box-sizing:border-box;caret-color:#000000;font-family:Avenir-Book;font-size:14px;line-height:22px;">Kaleyra uses Google Inc. to gather aggregate statistical information which are useful to evaluate the website utilization and the activities carried out by the visitor, stores the information collected by the cookie on servers that can be located in the United States or other countries.</p><p class="paragraph" style="margin-top:10px;margin-bottom:10px;box-sizing:border-box;caret-color:#000000;font-family:Avenir-Book;font-size:14px;line-height:22px;">Google reserves the right to transfer the information produced by its cookies to third parties where required by law or if the third party process information on its behalf. Google ensures not to associate the IP address with any other data held in order to obtain a profile of the user more detail.</p><p class="paragraph" style="margin-top:10px;margin-bottom:10px;box-sizing:border-box;caret-color:#000000;font-family:Avenir-Book;font-size:14px;line-height:22px;">Google reserves the right to transfer the information produced by its cookies to third parties where required by law or if the third party process information on its behalf. $('.owl-item.active').next().addClass('next-item');
});

function callback(){
setTimeout(function(){
$('.owl-item').removeClass('prev-item');
$('.owl-item').removeClass('next-item');
$('.owl-item.active').prev().addClass('prev-item');
$('.owl-item.active').next().addClass('next-item');
});
}
function getUrlVars() {
var url = window.location.href;
var vars = {};
if(url.split("?").length > 1){
var hashes = url.split("?")[1];
var hash = hashes.split('&');
for (var i = 0; i < hash.length; i++) {
params=hash[i].split("=");
vars[params[0]] = params[1];
}
}
return vars;
}

fields.push(obj);
}
});

$(document).ready(function () {
new WOW().init();
var a = 0;
if($('.map-section .content-row').length){
$(window).scroll(function() {
var oTop = $('.map-section .content-row').offset().top - window.innerHeight;
if (a == 0 && $(window).scrollTop() > oTop) {
$('.counter-value').each(function() {
var $this = $(this);
var countTo = $this.attr('data-count');
$({
countNum: $this.text()
}).animate({
countNum: countTo
},
{
duration: 2000,
easing: 'swing',
step: function() {
$this.text(Math.floor(this.countNum));
},
complete: function() {
$this.text(this.countNum);
//alert('finished');
}
});
});
a = 1;
}
});
}
$('[data-sidenav]').sidenav();
$(document).on('click', function (e) {
if ($('.sidenav').has(e.target).length > 0) {
return false;
}
else if ($('.hamburger').has(e.target).length > 0) {
if ($('.hamburger').hasClass('is-active')) {
$('.hamburger').removeClass('is-active');
}
else {
$('.hamburger').addClass('is-active');
}
}
else {
$('.hamburger').removeClass('is-active');
}

window.location = url;
});
});

'-o-transition' : 'all 0.4s ease'
});
},210);
}

$('.platform').removeClass('active');
$(this).addClass('active');
$('.platform-wrapper').hide();
var showBlock = id+'-wrapper';
$('.'+showBlock).show();
});

var $this = $(this);

var content = $this.attr('data-content');

var downloadTitle = $this.attr('data-download-title');

$('.whitepaper-form').show();

form.find('.card-content .heading4').text(title);
form.find('.card-content .paragraph').text(content);
form.find('.download-title').text(downloadTitle);
// globalForm.reset();
// form.reset();
form.modal('show');
});
